4024<h1>

40258 Types of Countertops: How to Choose the Best Countertop for Your Kitchen</h1>

4088<p>

4089As the primary working surface in your kitchen, countertops are a workhorse and a critical component of a functional kitchen. Countertops have even started taking the main stage as a statement piece in the kitchen&mdash;yet another reason why purchasing the right type of countertop is so essential!</p>

4090

4091

4092<p>

4093To choose the best countertop for your kitchen or other room in your house, here is a guide about the best kitchen countertop materials and how to coordinate them with your chosen aesthetic.</p>

4202<h2>

4203What to Consider When Purchasing Countertops</h2>

4204

4205</div>

4206</div>

4207</div>

4208</div>

4209<div class="">

4210<div class="styles-plugin-outer custom-outer-style-ROW-ad-dc-c-b-fbbdf">

4211<div class="styles-plugin-inner custom-inner-style-ROW-ad-dc-c-b-fbbdf">

4212<div class="Row-module_global__1T17H merce-row-container">

4213<div class="Layout-module_row__3IzXF merce-row">

4214<div class="Layout-module_omnimerse-column-sm-9__31QM8 Layout-module_marginTopOnSmall__2rO47 merce-column">

4215<div class="">

4216<div class="styles-plugin-inner custom-inner-style-COLUMN-ccce---b-ac">

4217<div class="merce-column-container">

4218<div class="styles-plugin-inner custom-inner-style-SINGLE_IMAGE-ddf-c--c-cacdbc">

4219<div class="SingleImage-module_singleImage__3fWXf ddf-c--c-cacdbc-singleImageAlignment">

4220<img class="ddf-c--c-cacdbc-image" src="https://img.vevano.com/WwrHmcLa6HmXsCkY6uE-qAsG2Q1AWBaHdNN68yWk7aU/rs:fill:0:0/q:80/aHR0cHM6Ly9jZG4udmV2YW5vLmNvbS9CbG9nL3Jlc291cmNlLWNlbnRlci90eXBlcy1vZi1jb3VudGVydG9wcy9uYXR1cmFsLXN0b25lLWNvdW50ZXJ0b3BzLmpwZw" alt="statement countertop kitchen" title="statement countertop kitchen"/>

4221</div>

4222</div>

4223</div>

4224</div>

4225</div>

4226</div>

4227<div class="Layout-module_omnimerse-column-sm-2__2dem_ Layout-module_marginTopOnSmall__2rO47 merce-column">

4228<div class="">

4229<div class="styles-plugin-inner custom-inner-style-COLUMN-ca--df-af-bbdba">

4230<div>

4231</div>

4232</div>

4233</div>

4234</div>

4235</div>

4236</div>

4237</div>

4238</div>

4239</div>

4240<div class="styles-plugin-inner custom-inner-style-TEXTBLOCK-baf-a-b-b-eca">

4241<div>

4242<div class=" TextBlock-module_textBlockContainer__X2cPA">

4243<div>

4244<p>

4245Here&rsquo;s what you should consider and look for while searching for durable countertop materials:</p>

4246

4247

4248<ul>

4249

4250 <li>

4251Stain resistance</li>

4252

4253 <li>

4254Heat resistance</li>

4255

4256 <li>

4257Scratch &amp; chip resistance</li>

4258

4259 <li>

4260Easy maintenance</li>

4261

4262 <li>

4263Appearance &amp; beauty</li>

4264

4265 <li>

4266Price</li>

4267

4268</ul>

4269

4270

4271<p>

4272Depending on the material, the countertop may require varying degrees of maintenance from regular cleaning tips and sealing. Different types of kitchen countertops may be prone or resistant to scratches, heat distortion or scalding, color fading, or absorption of fluids, which can lead to discoloration and stains. Knowing such things can help you pick the best kitchen countertop material that fits your functional and lifestyle needs.</p>

4273

4274

4275<p>

4276On top of being durable and easy to maintain, you likely want your countertops to look good within your kitchen too! That means coordinating the countertop style and color with flooring, cabinet and <a href="https://vevano.com/resource-center/cabinet-materials/" target="_blank">

4277cabinet materials</a>

4278, hardware, and other features to achieve your desired aesthetic.</p>

4279

4280

4281<p>

4282Like most other home features, you get what you pay for, so the more inexpensive the countertop material, the quality may also reflect that price point, and vice versa for more lofty price tags. Sometimes paying more upfront for countertop materials can save money in maintenance or replacement costs later on.</p>

4469<div class=" TextBlock-module_textBlockContainer__X2cPA">

4470<div>

4471<p>

4472One of the most popular and best kitchen countertop materials is quartz, or engineered stone. Quartz is incredibly sturdy and resistant to many of the issues that may plague other countertop materials, making it hygienic and easy to maintain.</p>

4473

4474

4475<p>

4476When most designers say quartz countertops, they are not 100% solid quartzite (which would be very high maintenance). Rather, quartz countertops are usually in the 90% range of pure quartz combined with other resins or composites to create a gorgeous, durable, non-porous surface for your countertops.</p>

4519<p>

4520Caring for quartz countertops is incredibly simple as they are one of the more low-maintenance countertop options available. Soap and water should do the trick. No sealing necessary.</p>

4563<p>

4564Available in a wide variety of colors and textures thanks to being an engineered stone, quartz is a very popular option for countertops due to its versatility and general appeal. It comes in veined, fine-grained, coarse-grained, or plain designs.</p>

4568Marble-look quartz is very popular as it features the beauty of natural marble but the resilience and lower maintenance of engineered stone.</p>

4768<div>

4769<p>

4770One of the most popular countertop materials, granite is a highly desirable countertop material for its durability, hardiness, and distinct appearance.</p>

4771

4772

4773<p>

4774Due to granite&rsquo;s popularity, it&rsquo;s more widely available and more affordable than it used to be, though it&rsquo;s still on the upper end of the spectrum since it&rsquo;s natural stone.</p>

4775

4777</div>

4796<div class="styles-plugin-inner custom-inner-style-COLUMN-ebc---ae-edadef">

4802<p>

4803<span style="font-size:18px;">

4804<strong>

4805Maintenance</strong>

4806</span>

4807</p>

4808

4809</div>

4810</div>

4811</div>

4812</div>

4813<div class="styles-plugin-inner custom-inner-style-TEXTBLOCK-fe-ab-f-bce-fffbb">

4814<div>

4815<div class=" TextBlock-module_textBlockContainer__X2cPA">

4816<div>

4817<p>

4818Natural stone countertops, whether granite, marble, or other stone, <a href="https://vevano.com/resource-center/care-for-stone-countertops/" target="_blank">

4819require regular maintenance and care</a>

4820. Granite is a porous stone, so it requires regular sealing. Depending on the strength of the sealant applied, a new sealant might need to be applied every 1-5 years. With proper care and sealing, granite can last decades.</p>

4821

4822

4823<p>

4824Some granite countertops will come professionally sealed and will likely not need sealing for up to several years. Sensa granite countertops are sealed with a proprietary protective coating that doesn&rsquo;t require annual sealing.</p>

4827</div>

4828</div>

4829</div>

4830</div>

4831</div>

4832</div>

4833</div>

4834</div>

4836</div>

4837</div>

4838</div>

4839<div class="">

4840<div class="styles-plugin-outer custom-outer-style-ROW-fae--fb-a-fdff">

4841<div class="styles-plugin-inner custom-inner-style-ROW-fae--fb-a-fdff">

4842<div class="Row-module_global__1T17H merce-row-container">

4843<div class="Layout-module_row__3IzXF merce-row">

4844<div class="Layout-module_omnimerse-column-sm-12__29AUW Layout-module_marginTopOnSmall__2rO47 merce-column">

4845<div class="">

4846<div class="styles-plugin-inner custom-inner-style-COLUMN-adfc-ec--e-eca">

4847<div class="merce-column-container">

4848<div class="styles-plugin-inner custom-inner-style-TEXTBLOCK-df-b-ac-c-fbecba">

4849<div>

4850<div class=" TextBlock-module_textBlockContainer__X2cPA">

4851<div>

4852<p>

4853<span style="font-size:18px;">

4854<strong>

4855Styling</strong>

4856</span>

4857</p>

4858

4859</div>

4860</div>

4861</div>

4862</div>

4863<div class="styles-plugin-inner custom-inner-style-TEXTBLOCK-ed-d-f-a-eda">

4864<div>

4865<div class=" TextBlock-module_textBlockContainer__X2cPA">

4866<div>

4867<p>

4868Granite comes in a wide variety of colors and patterns, so it&rsquo;s easy to personalize with your cabinets and flooring. Keep in mind that granite countertops can also feature multiple color tones, so pay attention to the shades to create the aesthetic you want.</p>

4869

4870

4871<p>

4872This in-demand stone can work with just about any style depending on the grain and colors. It&rsquo;s about coordinating similar or contrasting colors to pair countertops with cabinets and flooring.</p>

4873

4874

4875<p>

4876For example, black granite countertops pair very well with white cabinets to create a beautiful contrast in modern styles. Black granite countertops also have a home in traditional and rustic styles when paired with <a href="https://vevano.com/resource-center/wood-kitchen-cabinet-types/" target="_blank">

4877wood kitchen cabinets</a>

4878 or other organic elements.</p>

5069<p>

5070A very trendy and beautiful countertop material, marble countertops are another desirable natural stone option on the high-end side. Marble comes in two forms: honed and polished. Honed marble is porous and has a matte appearance, where polished marble has a protective surface with a shiny sheen.</p>

5074One way to reduce the cost of marble countertops is to use marble tiles instead of slabs.</p>

6544<h4>

6545<span style="font-size:18px;">

6546<strong>

6547Styling</strong>

6548</span>

6549</h4>

6550

6551</div>

6552</div>

6553</div>

6554</div>

6555<div class="styles-plugin-inner custom-inner-style-TEXTBLOCK-dcbc-ba-db-adc-becb">

6556<div>

6557<div class=" TextBlock-module_textBlockContainer__X2cPA">

6558<div>

6559<p>

6560Pigmenting can be added to the cement to change its shade. And once it&rsquo;s installed, concrete countertops can be acid-stained, polished, or stamped to be further personalized.</p>

6561

6562

6563<p>

6564Concrete countertops fit in nicely with industrial, modern, or rustic styles.</p>

6565

6566</div>

6567</div>

6568</div>

6596<div>

6597<h2>

6598Cost of Countertops</h2>

6599

6600</div>

6601</div>

6602</div>

6603</div>

6604<div class="styles-plugin-inner custom-inner-style-TEXTBLOCK-dbe-cf-f-ab-dbdc">

6605<div>

6606<div class=" TextBlock-module_textBlockContainer__X2cPA">

6607<div>

6608<p>

6609Depending on the material, countertops may cost between $20 - $300 per square foot, with luxury natural stones at the top range (like lava rock) and materials like laminate and tile at the lower end of the spectrum.</p>

6610

6611

6612<p>

6613It&rsquo;s not only the material that will determine how much your investment will be in your countertop renovation. Here are other accompanying factors will affect the cost of new countertops:</p>

6614

6615

6616<ul>

6617

6618 <li>

6619Amount and thickness of countertop material</li>

6620

6621 <li>

6622Installation and labor</li>

6623

6624 <li>

6625Custom countertop shapes or designs</li>

6626

6627 <li>

6628Removal of existing countertops</li>

6629

6630</ul>

6631

6632</div>

6633</div>

6634</div>

6635</div>

6636<div class="styles-plugin-inner custom-inner-style-TEXTBLOCK-fc-d-c-bc-fdea">

6637<div>

6638<div class=" TextBlock-module_textBlockContainer__X2cPA">

6639<div>

6640<p>

6641With this in mind, you can plan for a budget that allows you to purchase a durable and beautiful countertop that you can stay on top of maintaining.</p>

6642

6643</div>

6644</div>

6645</div>

6646</div>

6647</div>

6648</div>

6649</div>

6650</div>

6651</div>

6669<h2>

6670Choose a Countertop Material that Works Best for You!</h2>

6671

6672

6673<p>

6674We hope with guidance around the most sought-after countertop materials, their properties, maintenance requirements, style recommendations, and budget range, you can identify which countertop materials will work best for your home and kitchen.</p>
